SELECT  j.JOBSTATUS ,j.CREATEDATETIME,J.ANALYSIS,J.COMPLETED,J.INVOICESTART,J.ORIGINSTALLREF,J.FINALREMOVALREF,
J.[CONTRACT], J.IS_INVOICED,J.JOBREF,J.PROPERTYREF,JI.INVOICEDATE,JI.INVOICEDUPTO,JI.INVOICERAISEDTO
FROM JOBS J INNER JOIN JOB_INVOICEDUPTO JI ON JI.JOBREF = J.JOBREF 
WHERE J.ANALYSIS NOT IN ('REFIT','REM REFIT','OTHER') AND J.PROPERTYREF=338273
ORDER BY INVOICESTART DESC

SELECT DISTINCT J.JOBREF,j.PROPERTYREF ,j.ANALYSIS ,J.IS_INVOICED,I.THISINVOICEFROM,I.THISINVOICEUPTO FROM JOBS J ,INVOICESAVED I 
WHERE J.ORIGINSTALLREF =I.JOBREF AND J.COMPLETED < I.INVOICEDATE AND J.IS_INVOICED='N'
AND I.THISINVOICEUPTO BETWEEN '01-AUG-2014' AND '30-AUG-2014' AND J.COMPLETED BETWEEN '01-AUG-2014' AND '30-AUG-2014'

You can avail a non refundable (Loan) advance, out of your PF accumulations.

It's once in life time from the PF Account number that you currently have the accumulations in.

Benefit of Non - Refundable advance from the amount standing to the credit of member in the fund can be sanctioned for the following purposee :
1- Purchase of House.
2- Repayment of a loan for Housing.
3- Purchase of a house/site/flat under the housing scheme notified by the Central Provident Fund Commissioner.
4- Unemployument due to lockout or temporary closure.
5- Unemployment due to illness.
6- Marriage of self or of Daughter, Son , Sister, or Brother.
7- Education of Son or Daughter.
8- exceptional calamity.

The supporting documents will have to be attached for claiming the Non - Refundable advances.

=============================================

We can select all columns into the new table:

SELECT *
INTO new_table_name [IN externaldatabase]
FROM old_tablename

Or we can select only the columns we want into the new table:

SELECT column_name(s)
INTO new_table_name [IN externaldatabase]
FROM old_tablename

SQL SELECT INTO Example
Make a Backup Copy - Now we want to make an exact copy of the data in our "Persons" table.

We use the following SQL statement:

SELECT *
INTO Persons_Backup
FROM Persons
We can also use the IN clause to copy the table into another database:

SELECT *
INTO Persons_Backup IN 'Backup.mdb'
FROM Persons
We can also copy only a few fields into the new table:

SELECT LastName,FirstName
INTO Persons_Backup
FROM Persons

to find a coloumn in database
SELECT c.name AS ColName, t.name AS TableName,*  FROM sys.columns c JOIN sys.tables t
 ON c.object_id = t.object_id  WHERE c.name LIKE '%PHONE%'  
 
 SELECT COLUMN_NAME, TABLE_NAME   FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS   WHERE COLUMN_NAME LIKE '%VARNAME%'  
 
 select * from INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS where COLUMN_NAME like '%VARNAME%' order by TABLE_NAME  
   
 SELECT t.name AS table_name, SCHEMA_NAME(schema_id) AS schema_name,table_catalog,
 c.name AS column_name  FROM sys.tables AS t  INNER JOIN sys.columns c ON t.OBJECT_ID = c.OBJECT_ID
  WHERE c.name LIKE '%VARNAME%'  ORDER BY schema_name, table_name; 

select OBJECT_NAME(id), [text] from sys.syscomments where text like '%<>%'

--To select a text in DB
SELECT DISTINCT o.name AS Object_Name,o.type_desc 
FROM sys.sql_modules m 
INNER JOIN sys.objects o 
ON m.object_id=o.object_id 
WHERE m.definition Like '%LIVE_PROPS%'
----------------------------------------------------------DEALLOCATE Cursor
IF CURSOR_STATUS('global','myCursor')>=-1
BEGIN
 DEALLOCATE myCursor
END

You can use the sp_cursor_list system stored procedure to get a list of cursors visible to the current connection, and sp_describe_cursor, sp_describe_cursor_columns, and sp_describe_cursor_tables to determine the characteristics of a cursor.

CREATE PROCEDURE dbo.p_cleanUpCursor @cursorName varchar(255) AS
BEGIN

    DECLARE @cursorStatus int
    SET @cursorStatus =  (SELECT cursor_status('global',@cursorName))    

    DECLARE @sql varchar(255)
    SET @sql = ''

    IF @cursorStatus > 0
    	SET @sql = 'CLOSE '+@cursorName

    IF @cursorStatus > -3
    	SET @sql = @sql+' DEALLOCATE '+@cursorName

    IF @sql <> ''
    	exec(@sql)

END

--exec dbo.p_cleanUpCursor 'CUR_JOBS_UPDATE'

Dim combo = TryCast(DirectCast(sender, DataGridView).CurrentCell, DataGridViewComboBoxCell) 
        If combo Is Nothing Then 
            Return 
        End If 
--------------------------------
Public Sub GetSelectedInvoices()
        Try
            If grdBaseList Is Nothing Then
                Exit Sub
            End If
            If ListOfInvoiceSaved Is Nothing Then Exit Sub

            If ListOfInvoiceSaved.Count <= 0 Then Exit Sub

            _ListSelectedInvoiceSaved.Clear()
            With grdBaseList
                Dim i As Integer
                Dim CholumnChecked As Boolean = False
                For i = 0 To .RowCount - 1
                    CholumnChecked = .Rows(i).Cells("CHECKED").Value
                    If CholumnChecked Then
                        _ListSelectedInvoiceSaved.Add(Me.ListOfInvoiceSaved(i))
                    End If
                Next
            End With
        Catch ex As Exception
            Heirarchy.ExceptionHandler.HandleException(ex, False)
        End Try

Vat rate missing

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[UpdateTaxForInvoicesWithZero]    Script Date: 05/27/2013 16:30:17 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


/*----------------------------------------------------
Program Name 	: [UpdateTaxForInvoicesWithZero]
Program Type	: StoredProcedure
Description		: Function to update the INVOICES with zero tax
Author			: Pramod I Udakeri
Created Date	: 03/07/2012
Parameters		:
Name		Type		Input/Output	Description


Returns
Type	Description

Modification History
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Change	Date		By.		Histrory
Req ID
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
<CR #> 	<Date>			<Author>			<Reason for changes and  location of changes>
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EXEC UpdateTaxForInvoicesWithZero '1 Mar 13' ,'31 Mar 13' ,'20.00'
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateTaxForInvoicesWithZero](
@InvoiceFrom	DATETIME,
@InvoiceTo	DATETIME,
@TaxRate NUMERIC(10,2)
)
AS
BEGIN

	SET NOCOUNT ON;	

	UPDATE INVOICESAVED_HEADER SET HEADER_VATRATE = @TaxRate, HEADER_VAT = (HEADER_GOODSTOTAL * @TaxRate/100),
	HEADER_INVOICETOTAL = (HEADER_GOODSTOTAL + (HEADER_GOODSTOTAL * @TaxRate/100))
	WHERE HEADER_INVOICENUMBER IN (SELECT DISTINCT INVOICENUMBER FROM INVOICESAVED WHERE INVOICEDATE BETWEEN @InvoiceFrom AND @InvoiceTo AND ISNULL(VATRATE,0) = 0);

	UPDATE INVOICESAVED SET VATRATE = @TaxRate,VAT = (GOODSTOTAL * @TaxRate/100), INVOICETOTAL = (GOODSTOTAL  + (GOODSTOTAL * @TaxRate/100 ))
	WHERE INVOICEDATE BETWEEN @InvoiceFrom AND @InvoiceTo AND ISNULL(VATRATE,0) = 0

		
END

Query Update InvoiceSequence in Property_credit_notes

select * From PROPERTY_CREDIT_NOTES 
where --OFFICE = '002943770001' and
INVSEQ is null and CREDIT_NOTE_DATE between '01-MAY-2013' AND '31-MAY-2013'

declare @officeref nvarchar(20)
set @officeref = '002943770001'
update PROPERTY_CREDIT_NOTES  set invseq = 
(select CI.INVOICESEQUENCE from COMPANYINFO CI inner join customers c
on ci.REF = c.COMPANY inner join OFFICES O on O.CUSTOMERREF = c.CUSTOMERREF 
where o.OFFICE = @officeref) where OFFICE = @officeref and INVSEQ is null

-------------------------------------------------
Control character  	 Value  
Tab			 char(9) 
 
Line feed		 char(10) 
 
Carriage return		 char(13) 

char(13) is carriage return and char(10) is line feed. Different text editors/viewers will interpret it differently.
For example, in the SSMS output window, the following 3 does not show any difference.


Code Snippet
SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT 'HI ' + CHAR(13) + 'Jacob'

SELECT 'HI ' + CHAR(10) + 'Jacob'

SELECT 'HI ' + CHAR(13) + CHAR(10) + 'Jacob'

/*

---------

HI 

Jacob

---------

HI 

Jacob

----------

HI 

Jacob

*/ 

But if you copy it to NOTEPAD, you will see that the first two strings are displayed in a single line.
 A line break is inserted only for the last string.
If you want to generate a line break, it is a good practice to use CR and LF together. CHAR(13) + CHAR(10)

Cursor
USE AdventureWorks
GO
DECLARE @ProductID INT
DECLARE @getProductID CURSOR
SET @getProductID = CURSOR FOR
SELECT ProductID
FROM Production.Product
OPEN @getProductID
FETCH NEXT
FROM @getProductID INTO @ProductID
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN
PRINT @ProductID
FETCH NEXT
FROM @getProductID INTO @ProductID
END
CLOSE @getProductID
DEALLOCATE @getProductID
GO
------------------
DECLARE @TableName VARCHAR(255)
DECLARE @sql NVARCHAR(500)
DECLARE @fillfactor INT
SET @fillfactor = 80
DECLARE TableCursor CURSOR FOR
SELECT OBJECT_SCHEMA_NAME([object_id])+'.'+name AS TableName
FROM sys.tables
OPEN TableCursor
FETCH NEXT FROM TableCursor INTO @TableName
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN
SET @sql = 'ALTER INDEX ALL ON ' + @TableName + ' REBUILD WITH (FILLFACTOR = ' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(3),@fillfactor) + ')'
EXEC (@sql)
FETCH NEXT FROM TableCursor INTO @TableName
END
CLOSE TableCursor
DEALLOCATE TableCursor

Following are the documents required –
For all applicants:

1.	Latest passport sized photograph.
2.	ID proof – passport/driving license/Pan card/voter’s ID
3.	Residence proof (light bill/telephone bill/passport)
4.	Original attested bank statement of all accounts for 6 months
5.	Statement of all other loan accounts
6.	Fees/Cheque payable to HDFC Ltd.
7.	Past occupational History/Resume
8.	Investments in brief

For Employed:
1.	Original or attested salary slips for last 3 months

old fixed was not implemented properly
we have fixed this issue in our new logic

Refer excel sheet provided by Andrew from month end report. Property at 30 September, holding rental stocks, however there is no weekly rental in the report.

It’s not an issue, with old solution provided earlier has not updated the data for September ,we have run the job again for September with our new logic,
311152,3129,7199,7191

We are sharing the latest report of Sep(WeeklyRental_Sep_2013)
\\vpsfs04\data2\Shared\IT\Abhishek\UK  as the file size is too large 

if in case of INSTALL we calculate weekly rental for the completed date of the install, then in our scenario, when a property is removed completely with all rental items, we should not calculate weekly rental for the day it is removed. So, we should not have that property in the weekly rental tables, because weekly rental only shows properties which are live at that point with rental stocks

For example you can check Property ref 34871,whose removal is done on 14 th of Oct 2013,Bm charge this till the date of removal,so in weekly rental report data is present for this property till 14th oct 2013,but in Production you can check on 14 th Oct it shows ‘0’ Weekly rent, but on Prod copy you can see weekly rent(15.6) is calculted for this property.

---Usefull query
SELECT  j.CREATEDATETIME,J.ANALYSIS,J.COMPLETED,J.INVOICESTART,J.ORIGINSTALLREF,J.FINALREMOVALREF,
J.[CONTRACT], J.IS_INVOICED,J.JOBREF,J.PROPERTYREF,JI.INVOICEDATE,JI.INVOICEDUPTO,JI.INVOICERAISEDTO
FROM JOBS J INNER JOIN JOB_INVOICEDUPTO JI ON JI.JOBREF = J.JOBREF 
WHERE J.ANALYSIS NOT IN ('REFIT','REM REFIT','OTHER') AND J.PROPERTYREF=34871
ORDER BY INVOICESTART DESC

propriété

SELECT P.PROPERTYREF,
(CASE 
	WHEN J.HMJOBNO IS NULL THEN CAST(J.JOBREF AS NVARCHAR) 
	WHEN J.HMJOBNO ='' THEN CAST(J.JOBREF AS NVARCHAR) 
	ELSE J.HMJOBNO 
END)AS 'JOB NUMBER',
(ISNULL(P.FIELD1,'') + ' ' +  ISNULL(P.FIELD2,'')) AS 'ADDRESS',
(ISNULL(FIELD5,'') + ' ' +  ISNULL(FIELD6,'') + ' '+  ISNULL(FIELD3,'') + ' ' +   ISNULL(FIELD4,'')+ ' ' +  ISNULL(FIELD7,'')) AS 'PROPERTY LOCATION',
ISNULL((SELECT DBO.[GETATTRIBUTEVALUE](J.DEPOT,'',(SELECT  DSC.FIELD_ID FROM DYNAMIC_SCREEN DS , DYNAMIC_SCREEN_CONFIG DSC     
 WHERE DS.SCREEN_NAME='DEPOT' AND DSC.FIELD_ID LIKE '%STAMP%' AND DS.SYS_DYNAMIC_SCREEN_CODE=DSC.SYS_DYNAMIC_SCREEN_CODE))),'') As 'STAMP'
FROM PROPERTIES P inner JOIN JOBS J ON P.PROPERTYREF = J.PROPERTYREF and j.ANALYSIS='INSTALL' and J.PROPERTYREF =1105
order by J.JOBREF desc

SELECT * FROM  INVOICESAVED_VIEW_SPLITDDAC_SSRS AS I WHERE INVOICENUMBER IN (101390626) AND INVSEQ =2 ORDER BY I.JOBREF DESC


=CSTR(FormatNumber(reportitems!txtRunningValueGoodsTotal.Value + ((reportitems!txtRunningValueGoodsTotal.Value * First(Fields!HEADER_VATRATE.Value))/100) ,2)).ToString.Replace(".",",")+ " " + Fields!PDS.Value

=iif(Formatnumber(reportitems!txtLastPageCalculation.Value,2)<1, False,True)

Jayesh Dhale	SELECT C.REF,C.CompanyName , COUNT(DISTINCT I.PROPERTYREF) 'Total Properties',ROUND(SUM(I.GOODSTOTAL),2)  'Goods Total',COUNT(DISTINCT I.INVOICENUMBER)  'Total Invoices'

120691##] FW: UK005353 - Fabrick May 14 Schedule & Invoice



job lock release steps

To Unlock a job in BM

1) Please log off from application.
2) Login again.
3) Search for specific job and open the locked job.
4) Cancel the job.
5) Go back to the same job. 

This will resolve your issue

Dynamic insert script
SELECT 'Insert into INSPECTION_DETAILS values' + '('+ CAST(J.QID AS NVARCHAR) +  ',''' + CAST(J.QUESTION AS NVARCHAR(max)) + '''' +
','+'NULL' +',''' + CAST(isnull(J.ANSWER_DETAILS,'') AS NVARCHAR(max)) + ''''
+','+CAST(J.INSPECTREF AS NVARCHAR)+','+'NULL' +','+CAST(isnull(ltrim(rtrim(J.ANSWER1)),' ') AS NVARCHAR(max))+ ')'
FROM INSPECTION_DETAILS J WHERE j.inspectref=858979 order by J.QID

Dynamic Update script
SELECT P.STOCKREF,P.[CONTRACT],CT.CONTRACT,P.PERIODTYPE,P.LINENARRATIVE,P.SALESTAXFORCONTRACT,
CS.CUSTOMERNAME ,CS.CUSTOMERREF,
'UPDATE CONTRACTPRICEHEAD SET SALESTAXFORCONTRACT = 1 WHERE [CONTRACT] =' + ''''+ CAST(P.[CONTRACT] AS NVARCHAR) + ''''
+  ' AND STOCKREF =''' + CAST(P.STOCKREF AS NVARCHAR) + ''''
FROM CONTRACTPRICEHEAD P INNER JOIN CONTRACTS CT ON P.CONTRACT=CT.CONTRACT 
INNER JOIN CUSTOMERS CS ON CT.CUSTOMERREF  = CS.CUSTOMERREF
WHERE (P.SALESTAXFORCONTRACT =0 OR P.SALESTAXFORCONTRACT IS NULL) 

CONVERT(VARCHAR, INVOICEDATE,105)

1 )stockref NOT LIKE 'ANY%'
Stock ref should not be start from ‘ANY’
2)AND stockref NOT IN (SELECT stockref FROM stockanalysis_cols WHERE stockref IS NOT NULL)
Stock analysis should not be null
3)AND stockref NOT IN (SELECT stockref FROM RW_JOBSTOCK_ITEMS_JOB_noqty(@ajobref))
Stock ref should not be already present on that jobref
4)AND stock_analysis NOT IN (SELECT anal FROM exclanalysis(@ajobref))
Stock analysis should not be 
AND stock_qtyexpr IS NULL /*exclude calculated stock */

This will pad the varchar column v in table t to 30 characters:
update t 
set v = v+space(30-len(v))
where len(v) < 30

Notepad can be use as a Diary?
============================================ 
open a blank note pad file
 Type .LOG (caps) as the first line of the file, followed by a enter. Save the file and close it.

...3. Double-click the file to open it and notice that Notepad appends the current date and time to the end of the file and places the cursor on the line after.

4. Type your notes and then save and close the file.

5. Each time you open the file, Notepad repeats the process, appending the time and date to the end of the file and placing the cursor below it..!!!

Thanks!

INVOICE TO BE CANCELLED IMMEDIATELY!!!!!!

Select ji.JOBREF,ji.INVOICENUMBER,ji.INVOICEDATE,
(Select MAX(j.InvoiceDate) from InvoiceSaved j where j.InvoiceDate<ji.InvoiceDate and j.JOBREF = ji.JobRef) 'LASTINVOICEDATE',
ji.INVOICEDUPTO,ji.INVOICERAISEDTO,ji.PREVIOUS_INVOICE_CUTOFF into Temp_Job_InvoiceUpto_03DEc14
from JOB_INVOICEDUPTO ji Inner Join Jobs j on
ji.JOBREF = j.JOBREF
where ji.JOBREF in
(SELECT Distinct (JOBRef)  FROM INVOICESAVED WHERE INVOICENUMBER =14621)
Order By INVOICENUMBER Asc

The most important insight about how thread executions happen can be depicted by what is known assequence diagram. Here is an example from wikipedia

Ans:- Statement  ‘c’ is correct as in A1 algorithm the condition (if a[n]+b[n] < lowvalue) satisfied for 
        no. of student who got lowest mark overall (before + after).
 And in A2 algorithm the condition (if a[n]-b[n] >improvemost) satisfied for no. of student who   improved the most between b and a.


Ans:- Statement  ‘c’ (a[n]>=low and a[n]<=high) is correct, as we want to display the values of an array that falls between 2 input values, if we choose Statement ‘a’ and ‘b’ the or condition checks for the condition in this case if first condition is true it skips the next condition, for example we choose Low number as 2 and High number as 5 and we want to run above program with condition ‘a’ 
It will return 2,3,4,5 and same is the case for condition ‘b’.
Statement‘d’ will not return the values that fall between 2 input values, it will show out of that numbers.

State Transition Testing is a black-box test design technique in which test cases are designed to
execute valid and invalid state transitions.
It is also called as dynamic testing technique, which is used when the system is defined in terms
of a finite number of states and the transitions between the states.
The State Transition Testing is helpful where you need to test different system
transitions.

Total cost of ownership (TCO) is a financial estimate intended to help buyers and owners determine the direct and indirect costs of a product or system. It is a management accounting concept that can be used in full cost accounting or even ecological economics where it includes social costs.

Prod support  TL

"Response Time" is the time it takes to acknowledge a customer's issue in a non-automated way. It is measured from the time an Incident record is created, either by the customer via a HelpSU web submission or by the IT Service Desk or other support group manually creating a record, until the time that the customer is advised their problem has been received and is being addressed. The customer should be contacted either by phone or email and the Incident marked "In Progress".

https://itservices.stanford.edu/service/helpdesk/support/sla

Issue ID 61631 PRELIST A 0 BLOQUER AU SECOURS --1 hr
Preparation of MLR 4 BMV3 V4 NAV Data for 23Feb-27Feb report --1 hr



•The Resolution time will be the difference between the latest, most recent Resolution Date and Created date.

we have the SLA Response Time and Resolution Time configured to Auto-Populate calculating Submission Time + Resolution Time.  

Assuming the Situation: 
An agent opens a ticket for a call which they resolve on first contact.  The ticket is created in status Closed.  A SLA Due Date was auto-populated based on our Service Level Management Configuration (say 5 business days in the future).   In this case, we met the SLA and no SLA time was actually achived.  Let's then say a customer replies to this ticket 6 business days later, our configuration changes the status of this ticket to 'Re-Open' (an active SLA Status) and  immediately the SLA is violated (because the SLA Due Date was originally set to 5 days from ticket creation).   
 
I would expect it to be moved into an active SLA status with the remaining time on the original SLA.  However, it was confirmed by support that the SLA Due Date does not get updated based on a reply to a CLOSED status.

To handle such kind of Situation I will strongly encourge to use the Best Practice - Incident Resolution Workflow provides an ITIL-based best practice workflow to power the resolution of incidents. 
Best practices for incident resolution dictate that rather than closing the incident, the incident should have a state of Resolved. This state gives the service desk a mechanism to verify that caller is satisfied with the resolution, and that the customer agrees with closing the incident. This workflow is automatically enabled on instances. 
Users with the itil role or the itil_admin role have the capability to Resolve incidents with no option to close.
We can even set the access permission
.Closed incidents are read-only for non-administrators. 
.Incidents can only be reopened by users with the admin role. 
.Users with the itil role cannot reopen closed incidents. 
.ESS users have a Reopen Incident button on resolved Incidents. 

When an incident is set to a 'Resolved' incident state an email notification is sent to the caller. If the caller is satisfied with the resolution, no action is required on the caller's behalf. ServiceNow automatically closes the incident after 24 hours. If the caller is not satisfied, s/he can reopen the incident by clicking on the link within the email notification. This creates an outgoing Please Reopen email message. The user can add text to the outgoing email if they want to add any additional remarks. The Resolved incident is automatically reactivated and displays an Active status. 

If an incident is closed, an email is sent to the end user.So that it will get track in our record.

CREATE PROC SearchAllTables ( @SearchStr nvarchar(100) ) AS BEGIN

-- Copyright © 2002 Narayana Vyas Kondreddi. All rights reserved.
-- Purpose: To search all columns of all tables for a given search string
-- Written by: Narayana Vyas Kondreddi
-- Site: http://vyaskn.tripod.com + http://stackoverflow.com/questions/436351/how-do-i-find-a-value-anywhere-in-a-sql-server-database
-- Tested on: SQL Server 7.0 and SQL Server 2000
-- Date modified: 28th July 2002 22:50 GMT

DECLARE @Results TABLE(ColumnName nvarchar(370), ColumnValue nvarchar(3630))

SET NOCOUNT ON

DECLARE @TableName nvarchar(256), @ColumnName nvarchar(128), @SearchStr2 nvarchar(110)
SET  @TableName = ''
SET @SearchStr2 = QUOTENAME('%' + @SearchStr + '%','''')

WHILE @TableName IS NOT NULL
BEGIN
    SET @ColumnName = ''
    SET @TableName = 
    (
        SELECT MIN(QUOTENAME(TABLE_SCHEMA) + '.' + QUOTENAME(TABLE_NAME))
        FROM    INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES
        WHERE       TABLE_TYPE = 'BASE TABLE'
            AND QUOTENAME(TABLE_SCHEMA) + '.' + QUOTENAME(TABLE_NAME) > @TableName
            AND OBJECTPROPERTY(
                    OBJECT_ID(
                        QUOTENAME(TABLE_SCHEMA) + '.' + QUOTENAME(TABLE_NAME)
                         ), 'IsMSShipped'
                           ) = 0
    )

    WHILE (@TableName IS NOT NULL) AND (@ColumnName IS NOT NULL)
    BEGIN
        SET @ColumnName =
        (
            SELECT MIN(QUOTENAME(COLUMN_NAME))
            FROM    INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS
            WHERE       TABLE_SCHEMA    = PARSENAME(@TableName, 2)
                AND TABLE_NAME  = PARSENAME(@TableName, 1)
                AND DATA_TYPE IN ('char', 'varchar', 'nchar', 'nvarchar')
                AND QUOTENAME(COLUMN_NAME) > @ColumnName
        )

        IF @ColumnName IS NOT NULL
        BEGIN
            INSERT INTO @Results
            EXEC
            (
                'SELECT ''' + @TableName + '.' + @ColumnName + ''', LEFT(' + @ColumnName + ', 3630) 
                FROM ' + @TableName + ' (NOLOCK) ' +
                ' WHERE ' + @ColumnName + ' LIKE ' + @SearchStr2
            )
        END
    END 
END

SELECT ColumnName, ColumnValue FROM @Results
END

Hope you are doing well,
We will fixed this issue like the same way we did in the past.

The last Credit note which has been created is 81269.
The last invoice which has been created is 81270.
 
We will change the number of that invoice into the missing one and then set the number of the next invoice to 81270. 
So that you would have no gap in the invoice sequence.
 
So we will follow the below steps
Will map 81270 (to) --> 81239 and 
After that we will rset the counter to 81269 , so that next invoice number will start from 81270.
 
Please let us know if you are okay with this approach and also we would like to know do you also want to change the invoice date of that missing number?

Request you to stop creating new invoices until our reply.

It's wise to explain that you always put your job first, and schedule interviews before or after work, at lunchtime, during weekends if appropriate, and during personal time off. Many many happy returns of the day sweet heart..!
 
There are some job interview questions that are guaranteed to come up in most (if not all) of your job interviews — regardless of your industry, your experience level, and job type.

At the top of this list is the universal and much-dreaded classic: “Tell me about yourself.”


This question (or a variation like “Walk me through your background”) comes up in just about every job interview and many job searchers hate it.

They hate it because they get frustrated trying to decipher exactly what the interviewer is looking for. However, if you prepare properly, there’s no reason to dread this question.

In fact, this question is an opportunity — an opening for you to set the tone of the job interview and emphasize the points that you most want this potential employer to know about you.

Don’t waste the opportunity by simply diving into a long recitation of your resume. This also isn’t the time to mention that you love flamenco dancing and bingo (yes, I have seen candidates ramble on about hobbies and personal preferences many times and it’s a surefire way to make a weak first impression).

Instead, try a concise, enthusiastic response that summarizes your big-picture fit for the job. This is also a good opportunity to share some information about your proudest achievements and goals.

The Interviewer’s Perspective

What is the interviewer trying to achieve by asking you to “tell him about yourself”? Well, for the interviewer, it’s an easy and open-ended way to start the conversation.

His ultimate goal for this interview is to find out enough about you to decide if you’re a good fit for the job opening that he is being paid to fill. In most cases, he wants to like you. His life will be easier if he can find a great candidate quickly. However, he is also on guard because a bad hire will reflect poorly on his judgment and possibly be a mark against him when it comes time to ask for a raise or promotion or bonus.

He is hoping that this question will get you talking. This question is almost always asked first, perhaps right after some chit chat about traffic and the weather. As a result, his first impression of you will be all about your answer to this question. Your answer here will also set the tone for the interview and let you lead with your strongest selling points.

How to Nail “Tell Me About Yourself”

Think of it as your elevator pitch. An elevator pitch is a short summary used to quickly and simply define a product, service, or business and its value proposition. It answers the question: “Why should I buy/invest?” It should be concise enough to be delivered during a short elevator ride (to the 5th floor, not to the 105th floor).

You need an elevator pitch for yourself as a job candidate — and it should be customized for different opportunities. You must keep it focused and short, ideally less than a minute, and no more than 2 minutes.

You won’t be able to fit all of your great qualities and resume high points into 2 minutes, so you’ll have to spend some time thinking about how to present yourself in a way that starts the interview on the right note.

A great answer will address the following:

•What are your primary selling points for this job? This could be number of years of experience in a particular industry or area of specialization. You might also highlight special training and technical skills here. Focus on the qualifications in the job description and how you meet and exceed the requirements.
•Why are you interested in this position right now? You can wrap up your answer by indicating why you are looking for a new challenge and why you feel this role is the best next step.
The Skillful Formula for Answering This Question

I’ll share the “Tell Me About Yourself” formula that I teach to my interview coaching clients (and Big Interview members). There are three components:

1. Who You Are — Your first sentence should be an introduction to who you are professionally, an overview statement that shows off your strengths and gives a little sense of your personality too. This is not easy to do gracefully on the fly. It pays to prepare a bit in advance.

Good: “I’m an innovative HR manager with 8 years of experience managing all aspects of the HR function — from recruiting to training to benefits — for Fortune 500 companies.”

Concisely summarizes diverse background.

Bad: “Well, I grew up in Cincinnati. As a child, I originally wanted to be a fireman, then later became interested in dinosaurs. I excelled in the sciences from early on, placing first in my fourth-grade science fair. Funny story about that…”

Way too much information.

2. Expertise Highlights — Don’t assume that the interviewer has closely read your resume and knows your qualifications. Use your elevator pitch to briefly highlight 2-4 points that you think make you stand out.

Good: “I have spent the last six years developing my skills as a customer service manager for Megacompany Inc., where I have won several performance awards and been promoted twice. I love managing teams and solving customer problems.”

The emphasis here is on experience, enthusiasm, and proof of performance.

Bad: “My first job was as an administrative assistant for Macy’s in Fort Lauderdale, Florida. I learned a great deal in that role that served me well over the next 12 years. At the time, I wasn’t sure about my career path, so I next took a position selling real estate. It only lasted for six months, but I sure enjoyed it.”

Zzzzzzz. Nobody cares about your first job 12 years ago. You are starting with the least impressive part of your career and the interviewer is likely to tune out before you get to the good stuff.

3. Why You’re Here — End by telling them you want the position and why.

Good: “Although I love my current role, I feel I’m now ready for a more challenging assignment and this position really excites me.”

Concise and positive.

Bad: “Because of the company’s financial problems and my boss’s issues, I’m worried about my job’s stability and decided to start looking for new opportunities.”

Don’t be too candid or you risk coming across as negative. This answer also makes it seem like you’re interested in a job, any job — not this job in particular.

Remember: You will have time later to walk through your resume in more detail and fill in any gaps. Don’t try to squeeze in too much information or your interviewer WILL start to tune out.

A good interview is a dialogue, not a monologue. Keep it concise and give your interviewer the chance to dive in and ask questions.

Example Answer for “Tell Me About Yourself”:

“I have more than five years of experience as a technical project manager at top Wall Street companies. Most recently, I led the development of an award-winning new trading platform. I’m a person who thrives in a fast-paced environment so right now I’m looking for an opportunity to apply my technical exp and my creative problem solving skills at an innovative software company like this one.”

Coming to my educational qualifications,
Coming to my strength and weakness,
My strength is positive attitude, self-motivated and hard working. I don't want to expose my weakness I will try to overcome it always.
My short term goal is to get a job in a reputed company like yours and my long term goal is to be in respectable position in that organization.


Why You’re Here?
Although I love my current role, I feel I’m now ready for a more challenging assignment and this position really excites me.

-------------------------------------------- 1 jul
In Derived Column component instead of formatting the date sting in dd/mm/yyyy format, I formated the date string in yyyy-mm-dd format then type casted it to DT_DATE type in expression and the data type specified for the new column is unicode string[DT_WSTR] and then exported to Excel Component and excel picked it up nicely and date got displayed in dd/mm/yyyy format.

http://scn.sap.com/thread/1941281
The Actual problem is Regional Settings of the Operating System. 
I have changed the client machine's regional settings to English -  United kingdoms. 
The problem is in the regional settings English - United States. The English - United States was not able to identify the date format in excel which is exported as English - United Kingdoms


Solution: steps 1 and then 2

1) Select the date column. Under Data choose button Text to Columns. On first screen leave radio button on "delimited" and click Next. Unclick any of the delimiter boxes (any boxes blank; no checkmarks) and click Next. Under column data format choose Date and select MDY in the adjacent combo box and click Finish. Now you got date values (i.e. Excel has recognised your values as Date data type), but the formatting is likely still the locale date, not the mm/dd/yyyy you want.

2) To get the desired US date format displayed properly you first need to select the column (if unselected) then under Cell Format - Number choose Date AND select Locale : English (US). This will give you format like "m/d/yy". Then you can select Custom and there you can either type "mm/dd/yyyy" or choose this from the list of custom strings.

routes.IgnoreRoute("{resource}.axd/{*pathInfo}");
routes.IgnoreRoute("{*favicon}", new { favicon = @"(.*/)?favicon.ico(/.*)?" });

The route with the pattern {resource}.axd/{*pathInfo} is included to prevent requests for the Web resource files such as WebResource.axd or ScriptResource.axd from being passed to a controller.

The favicon route is to prevent the favicon to be mapped to a route.

create table tblemployee
(
EmployeeID int not null Identity(1,1) primary key,
Name nvarchar(20) not null,
Gender nvarchar(20) not null,
City nvarchar(20) not null
)

(
ID int not null Identity(1,1) primary key,
Name nvarchar(20) not null
)

(

http://localhost:52207/employee/details/2
user=sa;password=Secure04


string connectionString = ConfigurationManager.ConnectionStrings["DBCS"].ConnectionString

List<Employee> employees = new List<Employee>();

using (SqlConnection con = new SqlConnection(connectionString))
{
Sqlcommand cmd= new Sqlcommand("spGetAllEmployees",con);
cmd.CommandType = CommandType.StoredProcedure;
con.open();
SqlDataReader rdr = cmd.ExecuteReader();
whie(rdr.Read())
{
Employee employee = new Employee();
employee.ID = Convert.ToInt32(rdr["Id"])
employee.Name =rdr["name"].ToString();
employee.Gender =rdr["Gender"].ToString();
employee.City =rdr["City"].ToString();
employee.DOB =Convert.ToDateTime(rdr["DOB"]);

employees.Add(employee);
}

}

return employees;

create procedure spAddemployee
@Name nvarchar(20),
@Gender nvarchar(20),
@City nvarchar(20),
@DOB DateTime
as
begin
insert into tblemployeeBO (name,gender,city,DOB)values (@Name,@Gender,@City,@DOB)
end

public partial class department


//public ActionResult Edit([Bind(Include = "EmployeeDeptID,Name,Gender,City,DepartmentID")] employeedept employeedept)
        public ActionResult Edit([Bind(Exclude = "Name")] employeedept employeedept)
        {
            employeedept employeedeptfromdb = db.employeedepts.Single(x => x.EmployeeDeptID == employeedept.EmployeeDeptID);

            employeedeptfromdb.Name = employeedept.Name;
            employeedeptfromdb.Gender = employeedept.Gender;
            employeedeptfromdb.City = employeedept.City;
            employeedeptfromdb.DepartmentID = employeedept.DepartmentID;

            if (ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                db.Entry(employeedeptfromdb).State = EntityState.Modified;
                db.SaveChanges();
                return RedirectToAction("Index");
            }
            ViewBag.DepartmentID = new SelectList(db.departments, "ID", "Name", employeedept.DepartmentID);
            return View(employeedept);
        }

======================= raunak
The remote validator works by making an AJAX call from the client to a controller action with the value of the field being validated and optionally, the value of other fields. The controller action then returns a Json response indicating validation success or failure. Returning true from your action indicates that validation passed. Any other value indicates failure. If you return false, the error message specified in the attribute is used. If you return anything else such as a string or even an integer, it will be displayed as the error message.

GC
http://www.levibotelho.com/development/how-does-the-garbage-collector-work

Objects that implement the IDisposable interface can call this method from the object's IDisposable.Dispose implementation to prevent the garbage collector from calling Object.Finalize on an object that does not require it. Typically, this is done to prevent the finalizer from releasing unmanaged resources that have already been freed by the IDisposable.Dispose implementation.

Project Artifacts
In software development life cycle (SDLC), artifact usually refers to "things" that are produced by people involved in the process. Examples would be design documents, data models, workflow diagrams, test matrices and plans, setup scripts, ... like an archaeological site, any thing that is created could be an artifact.

In most software development cycles, there's usually a list of specific required artifacts that someone must produce and put on a shared drive or document repository for other people to view and share.

EFN=MINUS(# PLANNED EFFORT(HRS)#,# ACTUAL EFFORT(HRS)#)

SVN=DATEDIFF(5DAY,#ACTUAL START DATE#,#ACTUAL END DATE#)

SVD=DATEDIFF(5DAY,# PLANNED END DATE#,# PLANNED START DATE#)

EV=DIV(#EFN#,# PLANNED EFFORT(HRS)#)

SV=DIV(#SVN #,#SVD#)

Props optional parameter is available. If Props is not given it will disable the button as it does noe. 
For 1 it will enable the button, and 2:Hide button, 3:Unhide button, 0:Disable button. 
Third Parameter is Tooltip String, This can be used to give some more info on the button in both enable and disable case";

CREATEITEM(ConditionFormula,OwnerType,OwnerId,ItemType,FireGenerateEvent,LabelValueList)

__FORMULA__CREATEITEM(EQ(GETEFORMACTION(),CLOSE),Prj,#LS Of Defect.rowname.Owner ID#,Siu,Y,Name;;Defect close^^Description;;Test)

__FORMULA__CREATEITEM(EQ(GETEFORMACTION(),CLOSE),Prj,#LS Of Defect.rowname.Owner ID#,Siu,Y)


Creates a new eform item if the given condition is true OwnerType will be Org/Prj depending on the applicability 
of the eform OwnerId will be the corresponding OrgId or ProjectId ItemType will be the itemtype of the eform item 
FireGenerateEvent is an optional parameter Y/N for triggering the generate event on the item being created. 
LabelValueList will be a string of labelValue pairs separated by ^^ If not specified it will be Yes


__FORMULA__SETFIELDMANDATORY(EQ(#LS of Change Request.rowname.Workflow Stage#,Assigner),Impact,N)

Makes the given field(s) mandatory or not if the given condition is true for the current eform nonMandatory can have 
values 1/0 or Y/N. If nonMandatory is Y/1 and change event id fired, then it will make field Mandatory. 
otherwise it will make field nonManadatory. FieldLabelList is semi-colon separated. otherwise it is mandatory.

The different ways to create a project/program/template are:
create a project Using a Process Template: Process Template helps to model project/program/template so that a standard process can be 
followed in projects of similar type.

create a project Using a Personal or an Organization Data Template: An existing project/program/template is saved as a template and 
used while defining a project.

create a project Without using any template: Define a project that can have its own configuration.

You can also create Agile Projects for which the Agile module will be additionally available to manage the project 
based on the Agile methodology.

where you can click respective Timesheet and analyze causes for rejection and correct.

----------
Timesheet For filter will categorize the Timesheets as per the team member selection -- corresponding user’s Timesheet data is displayed.

By default logged-in user is selected

If there are no delegates or subordinates assigned then the filter is non editable filter

Search and select Subordinates or Delegated team members

-------
Project filter will display the Timesheets for projects as per search criteria or selection of projects
All projects in which you are team member and for which time tracking is enabled are listed.

By default Last Accessed Project will be shown

----
Work-Item Type filter lets you select only for the Work-Items assigned to you and as per specific eForms in the in the projects

Work-Item Status gets precise projects lists filtered on the basis of the Work-Item status.  
The applicable statuses are as follows:
All: This displays Timesheets for all three Work-Item statuses, viz. Pending, In Progress and Completed.
Pending: Comprises of only the Work-Items against which time has never been logged by the Timesheet user.
In Progress: In Progress item status displays the Work-Items against which time tracking has been done at least once.
Completed: This comprises of only the Work-Items that have been closed.
By default In Progress is selected to show the i Work-Items on which you are working.

----
Timesheet Status gets precise projects filtered on the basis of the Timesheet status.  The applicable Timesheet statuses are as follows:
Select All – All the following Timesheet Statuses are taken into account.
Not Filed – Timesheets for which effort logging has never been done
Saved – Timesheets which have been saved after effort logging
Corrected – Timesheets which have been corrected by Approvers
Routed – Timesheets which have been saved and routed for approval.
Rejected – Rejected Timesheets are listed here.

----
Week filter will display the Timesheet for the week to which the selected date belongs. Each time track is summarized on a daily basis and then is rolled-up to get the cumulative.

You can navigate to required date’s Timesheet by selecting the date from the Calendar widget.  This is based on the date or date range selected.

Past or future Timesheets can be generated through the Previous and Next navigation icons, in the Calendar widget. This shows the Timesheet for the previous or forthcoming week respectively

-------------- SLA
Apply SLA for Defects, Issues, Risks
Plan and define a SLA --
SLA details-SLA Domain
SLA details-SLA Category
SLA details-SLA Type
SLA details-Goal Unit

		
Add SLA Metrics
Through Add SLA Metrics icon, add and provide description. 

The added SLA work-item is shown in the SLA Metrics pane. 

Edit SLA Metrics
You can modify the SLA Metrics through the corresponding Edit SLA Metrics icon. 

Delete SLA Metrics
To remove the SLA Metrics, use the Delete SLA Metrics icon.

Define mapping between SLA metrics and the workflow stages to which the SLA is applicable

Define SLA Norms are conditions defined in the service level agreement (SLA). 

Defining the SLA Norms consists of 
Defining conditions
To define a condition for the required work-item, navigate to Add Condition >> Advanced Filter and define the Advanced Filter. 

You can manage filter criteria by adding new criteria or deleting not required criteria.
Defining Norms for the defined condition’s goal 

Enter the goal values in minutes (unit of time specified while defining the SLA) for default and respective defined conditions. 

If the condition for  the specific work-item is not met in the specified time interval then a non-compliance email gets triggered. 

SLA notifications need to be added before an SLA is activated. 

You can set notifications only for open items. 

SLA has to be compulsorily routed through all workflow stages for approval

Skip is not allowed --Skipping of workflow stages is not allowed for SLA

After SLA passes through the last workflow stage it can be activated. 

You can only have one SLA active at a time

You can apply the SLA to existing, open work-items on its activation

If the work-item type’s actual hours are within the goal, then SLA Compliance status is ‘Compliant’. 

When the time taken for completion of mapped workflow  stages of the work-item exceeds the goal, it becomes ‘Non-Compliant’.

The SLA’s response time tracking does not start if its workflow is not initiated. In such cases the SLA Compliance remains ‘Not Applicable’.

You can pause or resume a workflow to exclude it from the SLA tracking

You can define the list of common pause codes required for pausing the SLA in Master List.

Pause Notification attachment contains the pause date, time, reason code and relevant details.

======================= Test managment
Use the Test Unit export functionality to add/modify Test Units as required and import them back into Swift ALM
Copy Test Units through Batch Copy Test Units and reuse them after performing Batch Update
Build Requirement Traceability Matrix by tracking the traceability between Test Units and the Requirements
assign resources

Export and Import of Test Units
You can create a Test Script for every feature/functionality
Logically group the test units into test scripts and define the sequence of test execution in the Script Steps tab
You can add existing test units or create new ones for the test scripts

Operations permitted in Test Scripts are 
Copy, Reuse
Multiline Add, Edit, Delete 
Export, Import 
Re-sequence Test Units

You can perform Multiline Add Test Scripts, Edit, Delete, Import, Export and Print Test Scripts from the list toolbar icons

Reuse Test Units functionality
Use Delete Selected Test Units to remove selected Test Units from the Test Script
Resequence Test Units lets you rearrange the Test Units for execution

In a Test Event, add related test scripts to assess and test the required new or existing functionality.
(Add a new test event,Define the test event details)

You can assign single or multiple testers for a Test event

Import Test Scripts from the executing project or other projects too

View the summary of the Test Scripts in the Test event through Summary

To add additional Test Units to the Test Event within the Test Script, use Import Test Units.

For execution, select the test scripts, assign and schedule them. 
Specify Schedule Date, Owner and Executor for selected test scripts and Batch Schedule accordingly

Specify multiple executors in the workflow if you have many executors assigned for Test Units or Test Scripts

If the Test Case fails, update Fail status and save. Now you can link the failed test Unit to a defect

View Associated Defects if any by clicking the icon for the same.

__FORMULA__"Engagement Manager"
__FORMULA__"•	Handling the escalation from Client as well as offshore Team <BR>•	Handling new resource requirement in the Project <BR>•	Etc"

__FORMULA__"Project Manager"
__FORMULA__"•	Review the estimates <BR>•	Code review for critical objects <BR>•	Ensure delivery is as per schedule <BR>•	Ensure all requirement clarifications are closed <BR>•	Ensure all review/ test defects are tracked to closure <BR>•	Ensure test data is received from client on time <BR>•	Perform root cause analysis for critical defects, client reported defects, variance in schedule/ effort <BR>•	Ensure customer complaints (if any) are tracked to closure and corrective actions are implemented <BR>•	Etc"

__FORMULA__"Team Lead"
__FORMULA__"•	Development as per coding standards <BR>•	Execution of test cases/ scenarios <BR>•	Log defects <BR>•	Taking corrective actions <BR>•	Etc"

__FORMULA__"Onsite Coordinator"
__FORMULA__"•	Review the test cases <BR>•	Code review for critical objects <BR>•	Client coordination <BR>•	Introduction of new team members to client <BR>•	Etc"

__FORMULA__"Functional Consultant"
__FORMULA__"•	Participate in team meeting <BR>•	Prepare functional specs and carry out functional testing <BR>•	Fill up actual hours in PM tool application on daily/ weekly basis <BR>•	Fill up actual hours on project management tool on daily basis <BR>•	Report status to TL/ PM"

__FORMULA__"Technical Consultant"
__FORMULA__"•	Participate in team meeting <BR>•	Carry out coding as per Technical specification within defined schedule <BR>•	Adhere to client defined/ KPIT coding standards <BR>•	Close the review and testing defects <BR>•	Fill up actual hours in PM tool application on daily/ weekly basis <BR>•	Fill up actual hours on project management tool on daily basis <BR>•	Report status to TL/ PM"

__FORMULA__"Technical Reviewer"
__FORMULA__"•	Participate in team meeting, if required <BR>•	Should be well versed with client/ KPIT coding and documentation standards <BR>•	Perform technical review within defined schedule <BR>•	Log defects in RDF/ PM tool <BR>•	Re-review if required <BR>•	Fill up actual hours in PM tool application on daily/ weekly basis <BR>•	Fill up actual hours on project management tool on daily basis (if allocated on project)"

__FORMULA__"QAG"
__FORMULA__"•	Facilitate Project  team w.r.t QMS process implementation <BR>•	Perform SQA on monthly basis <BR>•	Impart QA related trainings"

setsegment header

__FORMULA__GETROWNAME()


SETSEGMENTHEADER(conditionFormula,SegmentName,OT,OID,IT,ItemName,SegmentHeaderFieldName,ExpandOrCollapse)

__FORMULA__SETSEGMENTHEADER(1,Receivables and Deliverable,Prj,OID,PMPI_f,ItemName,ABC,ExpandOrCollapse)

SETSEGMENTHEADER(1,Receivables and Deliverable,Prj,#LS.rowname.Owner ID#,#LS.rowname.Item Type#,#LS.rowname.Item Name#,ABC,ExpandOrCollapse)

This function is used to display segment header . This function accepts 8 parameter. 
First parameter is conditional formula (1/0). 
Second Parameter is SegmentName where header is to set. 
OT,OID,IT,ItemName refers to the eform instance where the header for that segment is configured. 
SegmentHeaderFieldName is the corresponding field for the segment that has the content to be displayed. 
ExpandCollapse will control if that header/footer section is 
collapsed/expanded by default.


SETSEGMENTHEADER(1,Details,Org,60002,HDFT_f,PMP HDFT 1,RTF Field 1,Expand)

PMP HDFT 1

RTF Field 1

Mention the receivables from the client and all deliverables that would be delivered to the client phase wise/ end of project

SETSEGMENTHEADER(conditionFormula,SegmentName,OT,OID,IT,ItemName,SegmentHeaderFieldName,ExpandOrCollapse)
__FORMULA__SETSEGMENTHEADER(1,Receivables and Deliverable,Org,80000,HDFT_f,PMP HDFT 1,RTF Field 1,Expand)

GETURL(1,I,Prj,80000,HDFT_f,ItemIdList,Documents,fullURL,Y,300,350,cssClass,extraParameter)

GETURL(conditionFormula,URLType,OwnerType,OwnerId,ItemType,ItemIdList,URLCaption,fullURL,OpenInNewTab,PopUpHeight,PopUpWidth,cssClass,extraParameter)

This function is used to display URL . This function accepts two parameter. 
First parameter is conditional formula (1/0). 
Second Parameter is URLType will be (E)xternal/(I)temIDList. 
Third parameter is a OwnerType. 
Fourth parameter is a OwnerId. 
Fifth parameter is ItemType. 
Sixth parameter is ItemIds List semicolon separated. 
Seventh parameter is URLCaption i.e. name on which URL has to be appended. 
Eighth parameter is URL which is needed if Custom URL needs to be used. 
Ninth parameter is OpenInNewTab which indicates whether to open URL in pop up mode or in new Tab(Y/N). 
Tenth parameter is PopUpHeight which is needed if Custom URL needs to be used. 
Eleventh parameter is PopUpWidth which is needed if Custom URL needs to be used.
Twelveth parameter is cssClass which is needed if Custom URL needs to be used on css class. 
Thirteenth parameter is the Extra parameter String which is needed on LOAD event of item to opened in event Details. 
For opening instance in Create or Edit mode pass thirteenth parameter as OpenInCreate^ or OpenInEdit^ at biginning of Extra parameter.

ISS2654 QA:Hidden fields is not retain its state after reloading of eform
Hi Jayesh, 
For handling your scenario wherever you have written HIDEFIELD or setlov you have to put ASSIGN logic considering combination of if 
based on any value is this field should be hidden or lov should be set and if not then what should be done. 
Take below literal for example. 
__FORMULA__HIDEFIELD(1,Current Customer,ASSIGN(NE(#LS.rowname.CustomerType#,Current),0,1)) 
In this way once change is made if it is hidden on next change it will unhide as well. Please configure this logic
